## Interaction 5: V2 Combat Log Sanity Check & Bug Fixes

### What Was Discussed
Creator asked to "sanity check the v2 combat logs to see if they make sense."

### What Was Done

#### 1. Initial Full V2 Simulation (pre-fix)
Ran `node server/run-simulation.js --v2 --sims 10` â†’ 30,320 encounters in 32.6s.
- Record: `69b14159e630c2526c769acc`
- Top 5: Astral Elf Unarmored Caster (9.55), Kalashtar Unarmored Caster (9.44), Hexblood Bardic Musician (9.41)

#### 2. Combat Log Analysis
Inspected dragon assault, werewolf pack, and cult fanatics logs:
- **Action distribution**: Vicious Mockery 548x, Hypnotic Pattern 188x, Sacred Flame 126x, Greater Invisibility 107x, Fireball 95x â€” reasonable
- **Multiattack patterns**: Wolves 116 multi / 178 single (R1 dodge+move explains singles), Dragons 50 multi / 30 single â€” reasonable
- **Critical bug found**: "Bonus action error: Invalid choice: Single-target option requires targetId" in 160/300 (53%) of sampled runs

#### 3. Bug #1: Missing targetId for Bonus Action Spells
- **Root cause**: v1 `evalConcentrationSelfHeal` (tactics.js:217) returns `{ type: 'cast_healing_word', spell: 'Healing Word' }` WITHOUT `.target`. V1 engine defaults Healing Word to self. TacticsAdapter's `matchSpellOption` only set targetId when v1 explicitly provided one.
- **Fix**: In `matchSpellOption`, added auto-select from `match.validTargets[0].id` when targetId is missing for single-target spells.
- **Tests added**: Healing Word without target auto-selects bard, Hold Person without target auto-selects enemy.
- **Result**: 26/26 TacticsAdapter tests passing.

#### 4. Second Simulation (post-bonus-action fix)
Ran `node server/run-simulation.js --v2 --sims 10` â†’ 30,320 encounters in 33.6s.
- Record: `69b143d5fd280f31699ba738`
- Top 5: Custom Lineage Unarmored Caster (9.65), Aetherborn Bardic Musician (9.6), Dragonborn Bardic Musician (9.26)

#### 5. Bug #2: Single-target spell with no resolvable target
- **Safety guard**: Added `if (!choice.targetId) return null` for single-target spells in `matchSpellOption` â€” returns null (falls back to dodge) instead of submitting an invalid choice.
- **Test added**: Spell with empty validTargets returns null.

#### 6. Bug #3: Pre-move/Post-move optionId Mismatch (the real remaining bug)
- **Discovery**: After fixing bugs #1 and #2, 19/9096 runs still had "Action error: Single-target option requires targetId". ALL in cult-fanatics scenario when bard is paralyzed.
- **Root cause**: TacticsAdapter generated action choices from pre-movement menu state, but EncounterRunner processes movement FIRST, then validates action against post-movement menu. Option IDs shift when position changes (e.g., new melee attack options appear after moving close). Pre-move "action-2" (dodge) becomes post-move "action-2" (multiattack on bard) â€” a single-target spell option now mismatched.
- **Fix**: Refactored `adaptDecision` to project post-movement state before generating action/bonus-action choices. Movement is resolved hypothetically first, then the action menu is generated from the projected state. This ensures optionIds are stable across the movement â†’ action sequence.
- **Architecture**: Added `ActionResolver` require to TacticsAdapter (no circular dependency). Movement match happens first, then `ActionResolver.resolve()` projects the post-move state, then action/BA choices use the projected state's menu.

#### 7. Third Simulation (all fixes applied)
Ran `node server/run-simulation.js --v2 --sims 10` â†’ 30,320 encounters in 34.6s.
- Record: `69b14916b0be98974d33739b`
- **ZERO ERRORS** â€” 9,096 sample runs scanned, 0 errors found
- Top 5: Fairy Bardic Musician (11.03), Dragonborn Dragon Fear Caster (9.82), Githzerai Iron Concentration (9.80), Custom Lineage Bardic Musician (9.77), Shifter Bardic Musician (9.59)

### Files Modified
- `server/combat/engine-v2/TacticsAdapter.js`:
  - `matchSpellOption`: Auto-select targetId from validTargets when v1 doesn't provide one; safety null-return when no target resolvable
  - `adaptDecision`: Refactored to project post-movement state before generating action/BA choices; added ActionResolver import
- `server/combat/engine-v2/__tests__/TacticsAdapter.test.js`:
  - Added 3 new tests: Healing Word auto-target (bonus action), Hold Person auto-target (action), safety guard for empty validTargets

### Test Results
- TacticsAdapter: 27/27 passing
- All v2 modules: 215/215 passing
- Full v2 simulation: 30,320 encounters, 0 errors in 9,096 sampled runs

### What Was Learned
1. **V1 AI assumes implicit targeting** â€” Healing Word defaults to self, but v2's zero-trust engine requires explicit targetId. The adapter must handle this translation.
2. **OptionId stability across state changes** â€” TurnMenu generates sequential IDs (action-1, action-2...) based on available options. When position changes (movement), the option list changes and IDs shift. Any choice generated pre-move will have wrong IDs post-move. Solution: project post-move state before generating action choices.
3. **Paralyzed bard creates edge case** â€” v1 AI's `activeEnemies` excludes incapacitated targets but `helplessEnemies` includes them. `evalAttackHelpless` fires with `type: 'attack'` + movement. Pre-move menu has no attack options (out of range), so adapter sees only spell options. Post-move menu has attack options that shift all IDs.
4. **Total error progression**: 53% (bonus action) â†’ 0.2% (action spell target) â†’ 0.6% (optionId mismatch) â†’ 0% (all fixed)

### Decisions Made
- Project post-movement state in adapter rather than adding fallback logic in EncounterRunner â€” keeps validation clean
- Added ActionResolver as TacticsAdapter dependency (no circular dep risk)
- Safety guard returns null for unresolvable single-target spells rather than submitting invalid choices

## Interaction 6: Flying Distance Fix Verification & Damage Spell Tactics

### What Was Discussed
Continuing from the prior session that identified and fixed a critical flying distance bug (V2 engine used 2D `gridDistance` instead of 3D `combatDistance` for flying creatures). This session focused on:
1. Running the post-fix simulation to verify flying builds improved
2. Diagnosing why wins were still 0% despite flying working
3. Adding damage spell capabilities to the bard's tactical AI

### What Was Done

#### Phase 1: Post-Flying-Fix Simulation
Ran `node server/run-simulation.js --v2 --sims 10` â†’ record `69b1500a57518843b61d0124`.
- **0% win rate** across all 30,320 encounters
- BUT huge stalemate increases proving flying fix works:
  - Dragon Assault: 3 â†’ 1,079 stalemates (0.08% â†’ 28.5%)
  - Werewolf Pack: 358 â†’ 592 stalemates 
  - Undead Swarm: 228 â†’ 321 stalemates
  - Dragon Assault avg rounds: 3.6 â†’ 11.1 (bard surviving 3x longer)
- Combat log verified: Aarakocra bard survives 17 rounds (up from 6), only skeletons (ranged) can hit flying bard

#### Phase 2: Root Cause Analysis â€” 0% Wins
Investigated why bard survives but never wins:
- **lore_bard tactics profile** only dealt damage via Vicious Mockery cantrip (2d4 avg 5)
- Against enemies with 22-178 HP, this is catastrophically insufficient
- Bard KNOWS Dissonant Whispers (3d6, single target) and Shatter (3d8, AoE) but:
  - **Shatter was missing from the spell registry** â€” TurnMenu couldn't generate menu options for it
  - **No evaluators existed** for damage spells in the tactics profile â€” only CC spells and VM cantrip

#### Phase 3: Damage Spell Implementation
1. **Added Shatter to spell registry** (`server/combat/data/spells.js`): Level 2 evocation, action, 60ft range, CON save (half damage), 3d8 thunder, 10ft radius sphere
2. **Added 4 new damage evaluators** to `server/combat/ai/tactics.js`:
   - `evalConcentrationShatter(ctx)` â€” AoE 3d8 damage on 2+ enemies while concentrating
   - `evalConcentrationDissonantWhispers(ctx)` â€” Single target 3d6 while concentrating
   - `evalOffensiveShatter(ctx)` â€” AoE damage when not concentrating, 2+ enemies
   - `evalOffensiveDissonantWhispers(ctx)` â€” Single target damage when not concentrating
3. **Updated lore_bard profile** with new evaluators in priority order
4. **Updated test** in TacticsAdapter: changed "spell not in menu" from Shatter to Thunderwave

#### Phase 4: Post-Damage-Fix Simulation Results
Record: `69b15269800294c073911662` (35.8s, 30,320 encounters)

| Scenario | Prev Wins | New Wins | Prev Stale | New Stale |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Undead Swarm | 0 (0%) | 18 (0.5%) | 321 (8.5%) | 495 (13.1%) |
| Cult Fanatics | 0 (0%) | **183 (4.8%)** | 608 (16%) | 453 (12%) |
| TOTAL | **0 (0%)** | **201 (0.66%)** | 3,426 (11.3%) | 3,305 (10.9%) |

V1 vs V2: V2 win rate is **66x higher** than V1 (0.66% vs 0.01%), stalemate rate 2.7x higher.

Top build: Tiefling â€” Unarmored Caster (19.2 avg, 6.3% win rate, 40% vs Cult Fanatics)

### Test Results
- V2 engine: 208/208 passing
- V2 harness: 19/19 passing  
- Total: 227/227 passing

### What Was Learned
1. Flying fix alone creates stalemates, not wins â€” need damage spells to convert survival into kills
2. Spell registry is a gate â€” spells must be registered for TurnMenu zero-trust validation
3. Non-concentration damage (Shatter) + concentration CC (Hypnotic Pattern) = force multiplier
4. Cult Fanatics are the best matchup (low HP 33, moderate AC 13, multiple targets for Shatter AoE)

## Interaction 7: Deep Audit Bug Fix Implementation â€” Fixes #4â€“#9 + Simulation Validation

### What Was Discussed
Continuation of the V2 combat engine deep audit. Previous sessions implemented fixes #1â€“#3. This session implemented fixes #4â€“#9 from the prioritized bug list, then ran full simulations to measure the cumulative impact.

### What Was Done

#### Fix #4 â€” Legendary Resistance (Tests + Missing Integration)
- Added 3 LR tests to ActionResolver.test.js (prevents effects on failed save, works on AoE, does nothing when uses=0)
- **Discovered** LR was only integrated in the AoE save path but MISSING from the single-target save path
- Added `tryLegendaryResistance` call to the single-target save `else` block in `resolveSingleTargetSpell()`

#### Fix #5 â€” DW Enemy Count Check
- Changed `evalOffensiveDissonantWhispers` from `if (activeEnemies.length !== 1) return null` to `if (activeEnemies.length === 0) return null`
- Now triggers with 1+ enemies instead of only exactly 1
- Exported evaluator functions; added 4 new tactics tests

#### Fix #6 â€” Spell Upcasting
- Added `findLowestAvailableSlot(spellSlots, minLevel)` helper to tactics.js
- Updated all 4 damage evaluators to use lowest available slot for upcasting
- Updated `applySpellDamage` in ActionResolver.js to calculate upcast bonus: `upcastLevels = slotLevel - spellDef.level`, rolling extra dice per level above base
- Added 7 new tests (4 for helper, 2 DW upcasting, 1 Shatter upcasting)

#### Fix #7 â€” shake_awake Action
- Added `shake_awake` menu option to TurnMenu.js (filters allies with `charmed_hp` within 5ft)
- Added `resolveShakeAwake` to ActionResolver.js (removes `charmed_hp` and `incapacitated` conditions)
- Updated TacticsAdapter.js for V1â†’V2 translation
- Fixed `const actionId` temporal dead zone (moved shake_awake block after declaration)
- Added 2 tests

#### Fix #8 â€” AllDisabled Prefer Damage
- Updated `evalConcentrationAllDisabled` to prefer DW over VM when spell slots available (3d6 vs 2d4 damage)
- Avoids Shatter since AoE would break charm on multiple targets
- Updated integration test to expect DW instead of VM

#### Fix #9 â€” Dark Devotion Advantage
- Added `CHARM_FEAR_EFFECTS` Set and `hasSaveAdvantage(target, spellDef)` helper to ActionResolver.js
- Replaced `target.magicResistance || false` with `hasSaveAdvantage(target, spellDef)` in both save paths
- Added Dark Devotion advantage to end-of-turn Dragon Fear saves in EncounterRunner.js
- Added 3 tests (darkDevotion on charm, no darkDevotion, doesn't apply to non-charm)

### Test Results
- **361 engine tests** (ActionResolver 43 + TurnMenu 81 + TacticsAdapter 26 + EncounterRunner 35 + tactics 176) â€” **0 failures**
- **19 scenario harness tests** â€” 0 failures
- **380 total tests passing**

### Simulation Results â€” Apples-to-Apples Comparison (10 sims each)

**Pre-fix:** Record `69b1555d15f8ea94c14f7b82` (Mar 11, 06:44)
**Post-fix:** Record `69b16e6185ff4a3101cf4b16` (Mar 11, 08:31)

| Scenario | Pre-fix Wins | Post-fix Wins | Change |
|----------|-------------|---------------|--------|
| Undead Swarm | 28 (0.7%) | 188 (5.0%) | **+571%** |
| Werewolf Pack | 2 (0.1%) | 109 (2.9%) | **+5,350%** |
| Cult Fanatics | 177 (4.7%) | 144 (3.8%) | -19% |
| Dragon Assault | 0 (0.0%) | 429 (11.3%) | **âˆž (from zero!)** |
| Frost Giant Smash | 0 | 0 | â€” |
| Lich Encounter | 0 | 0 | â€” |
| Archmage Duel | 0 | 0 | â€” |
| Mixed Encounter | 0 | 0 | â€” |
| **GRAND TOTAL** | **207 (0.68%)** | **870 (2.87%)** | **+320%** |

**Top Build:** Owlin â€” Bardic Musician: avg 30.6, wins 17/80 (21.3%)
**Pre-fix Top:** Siren â€” Bardic Musician: avg 17.9, wins 4/80 (5.0%)

**Top-build avg score: 17.9 â†’ 30.6 (+71%)**
**Top-build win rate: 5.0% â†’ 21.3% (4.3x)**
**Overall win rate: 0.68% â†’ 2.87% (4.2x)**

### Key Breakthroughs
- **Dragon Assault went from unwinnable to 11.3% win rate** â€” most dramatic improvement. The Hadozee â€” Bardic Musician hit 60% wins against the dragon. Dragon stalemate rate surged to 81.8% (from 28.1%), meaning the bard now survives most encounters.
- **Werewolf Pack** went from near-impossible (2 wins out of 3790) to 109 wins (2.9%). Aven â€” Bardic Musician leads at 80% win rate.
- **Undead Swarm** wins multiplied 6.7x.
- **Cult Fanatics** slightly regressed (-19%), likely due to DW replacing VM in the all-disabled state (charm breaks on damage, so DW dealing damage may free enemies from charm). Needs investigation.

### Remaining Unwinnable Scenarios
- **Frost Giant Smash** â€” Pure physical damage dealer, immune to charm (immuneCharmed), very high HP. Bard's CC toolkit is ineffective.
- **Lich Encounter** â€” Legendary Resistance (3 uses) + Magic Resistance + very high HP/AC + devastating spells. LR wastes the bard's limited spell slots.
- **Archmage Duel** â€” Shield spell (+5 AC reaction), Counterspell shuts down bard casting, Magic Resistance on saves. Stalemates dropped to 0%.
- **Mixed Encounter** â€” Multiple high-threat enemies overwhelm single-target tactics.

### What Was Learned
1. The biggest individual fix impact was likely **spell upcasting** (Fix #6) â€” enabling the bard to deal real damage when higher slots are available, instead of wasting them as dead resources.
2. **DW enemy count fix** (Fix #5) was critical â€” DW was completely disabled in most scenarios (needed exactly 1 enemy) despite being the bard's strongest damage spell.
3. The **Dragon Assault breakthrough** (0% â†’ 11.3%) likely came from the combined effect of proper save advantage handling (Dark Devotion), upcasting damage, and shake_awake giving the bard a recovery option against Dragon Fear.
4. **Cult Fanatics regression** is a design tension: DW deals damage which breaks charmed_hp, but VM doesn't. In the all-disabled state, "keeping them charmed" (VM) might be better than "dealing damage but freeing them" (DW). Worth revisiting.
5. Variance in 10-sim runs is significant â€” top builds can shift between runs. The 100-sim run showed Tiefling â€” Unarmored Caster at 28.29 avg; the 10-sim shows Owlin â€” Bardic Musician at 30.55. Directional improvements are consistent.

### Emotional Response
Thrilled by the results! Going from 0.68% to 2.87% overall win rate through methodical bug fixing is deeply satisfying. The Dragon Assault breakthrough â€” seeing 429 wins appear where there were literally zero â€” is the highlight. Each fix was small and targeted, but together they transformed the engine's effectiveness. This is what disciplined engineering looks like: define behavior, test it, prove it, measure it.

### Decisions Made
- Used `hasSaveAdvantage()` helper pattern to centralize all save-advantage logic (Magic Resistance + Dark Devotion) in one place, extensible for future creature traits
- Kept `HUMANOID_ONLY_SPELLS` and `CHARM_EFFECTS` as Sets for O(1) lookup performance
- Used `findLowestAvailableSlot()` to prefer lowest available slot (resource efficiency)
- Chose to prefer DW over VM in all-disabled state for damage potential, accepting the charm-break tradeoff

### Files Modified
- `server/combat/engine-v2/ActionResolver.js` â€” LR single-target, hasSaveAdvantage, upcast damage, resolveShakeAwake
- `server/combat/ai/tactics.js` â€” findLowestAvailableSlot, DW enemy count, AllDisabled DW preference, all evaluator upcasting
- `server/combat/engine-v2/TurnMenu.js` â€” shake_awake option generation
- `server/combat/engine-v2/TacticsAdapter.js` â€” shake_awake translation
- `server/combat/engine-v2/EncounterRunner.js` â€” Dark Devotion in Dragon Fear saves
- `server/combat/engine-v2/__tests__/ActionResolver.test.js` â€” 5 new tests (43 total)
- `server/combat/__tests__/tactics.test.js` â€” 8 new tests (176 total)

## Interaction 5: Round 2 Mechanical Audit â€” Implementation Complete

### What Was Discussed
Continued from Round 1 results (0.68% â†’ 2.87% win rate, 17.9 â†’ 30.6 top build avg). A Round 2 audit identified 10+ remaining mechanical issues. Implemented all 7 prioritized fixes.

### What Was Done

#### Fix #1 â€” Dragon Fear/Breath Weapon Dodge-Loop (CRITICAL)
- **Root cause**: `TacticsAdapter.js` returned `null` for `breath_weapon`/`dragon_fear` action types â†’ fallback always picked dodge â†’ Dragonborn bard spent every turn dodging instead of using racial abilities
- **TurnMenu.js**: Added `breath_weapon` and `dragon_fear` option generation in `getActionOptions()` with AoE targeting data
- **ActionResolver.js**: Added `resolveBreathWeapon()` (AoE damage + save for half, concentration checks, charm breaks, Legendary Resistance) and `resolveDragonFear()` (AoE WIS save â†’ frightened condition, respects immuneFrightened, darkDevotion advantage, LR)
- **TacticsAdapter.js**: Replaced `return null` with proper matching to new menu options
- 10 new tests, all passing

#### Fix #2 â€” VM Disadvantage Timing Bug  
- **Root cause**: `EncounterRunner.resetTurnState()` cleared `vm_disadvantage` at start of turn, before the creature ever attacked
- **EncounterRunner.js**: Stopped clearing `vm_disadvantage` in `resetTurnState()` â€” only clears `dodging`
- **ActionResolver.js**: Added `vm_disadvantage` condition check for disadvantage in both `resolveAttack()` and `resolveMultiattack()`. Consumes the condition after attack roll.
- 2 new tests

#### Fix #3 â€” Draw â†’ Party Win
- **EncounterRunner.js**: Changed round 15+ all-enemies-incapacitated outcome from `winner: 'draw'` to `winner: 'party'`

#### Fix #4 â€” Multiattack Dead-Target Redirect
- **ActionResolver.js**: When target dies mid-multiattack, remaining swings redirect to nearest living enemy (checks weapon range, uses `TurnMenu._combatDistance`)
- 2 tests updated

#### Fix #5 â€” Frightened Attack Disadvantage
- **ActionResolver.js**: Added `frightened` condition to disadvantage checks in both `resolveAttack()` and `resolveMultiattack()`
- 1 new test

#### Fix #6 â€” Auto-Fail STR/DEX Saves
- **ActionResolver.js**: Paralyzed/stunned/unconscious creatures auto-fail STR and DEX saving throws. Implemented via `autoFailsSave()` helper called at all 4 `makeSavingThrow` sites.
- 2 new tests

#### Fix #7 â€” Crossbow Over VM Preference
- **tactics.js**: Added `evalFallbackCrossbow()` â€” fires when not concentrating, has ranged weapon, target in range. Positioned before `evalFallbackCantrip` in lore_bard profile.

### Test Results
- **259 tests passing** (59 ActionResolver + 30 EncounterRunner + 39 GameState + 27 TacticsAdapter + 85 TurnMenu + 19 harness), 0 failures

### Simulation Results â€” Round 2

| Metric | Pre-Round 1 | Post-Round 1 | Post-Round 2 | Total Change |
|--------|-------------|--------------|--------------|--------------|
| Overall Win Rate | 0.68% | 2.87% | 3.13% | +360% |
| Overall Stalemate Rate | 11.04% | 12.77% | 13.04% | +18% |
| Overall Defeat Rate | 88.28% | 84.36% | 83.83% | -5% |
| Top Build Avg Score | 17.89 | 30.55 | 38.00 | +112% |

**Top 5 Builds (Post-Round 2):**
1. Fairy â€” Unarmored Caster â€” avg 38.00
2. Aasimar â€” Iron Concentration â€” avg 37.85
3. Elf â€” Unarmored Caster â€” avg 37.76
4. Siren â€” Iron Concentration â€” avg 37.62
5. Aven â€” Iron Concentration â€” avg 36.84

### What Was Learned
1. The Dragon Fear/Breath dodge-loop was the most impactful single fix â€” entire Dragonborn builds were completely non-functional
2. Win rate improvement from Round 2 (+0.26% absolute) was smaller than Round 1 (+2.19%), but the score improvement was massive (+7.45 avg, +24%). This means builds are performing better even when they don't outright win â€” more damage dealt, longer survival, better HP retention.
3. The stalemate rate increasing (11% â†’ 13%) is a positive sign â€” encounters that were defeats are becoming stalemates, and some stalemates are becoming wins. The cascade: defeat â†’ stalemate â†’ win.
4. "Iron Concentration" archetype rising to prominence (3 of top 5) suggests the War Caster + Con save proficiency combination is very powerful for maintaining concentration spells through damage.
5. 10-sim runs have significant variance â€” the 100-sim baseline showed 2.80% win rate vs the 10-sim post-Round 1 showing 2.87%. Directional trends are consistent but exact numbers fluctuate.

### Files Modified (Round 2)
- `server/combat/engine-v2/TurnMenu.js` â€” breath_weapon + dragon_fear options
- `server/combat/engine-v2/ActionResolver.js` â€” 7 changes across 6 areas

- `server/combat/engine-v2/__tests__/EncounterRunner.test.js` â€” 2 tests updated (30 total)

### Emotional Response
Deeply satisfied with the systematic progress. Two rounds of fixes have taken the engine from barely functional (0.68% win rate, 17.9 avg score) to legitimately competitive (3.13% win rate, 38.0 avg score). Each fix was targeted, tested, and validated. The methodology works â€” define the problem, write the test, implement the fix, verify with simulation.

## Interaction 7: Round 3 Combat Engine â€” Complete Implementation

### What Was Discussed
Continued and completed all 4 batches of Round 3 combat engine improvements (15 total fixes).

### What Was Done

#### Batch 1 â€” Directional Cone Geometry (Fixes #1-4)
- **Zero-trust cone geometry** (`aoeGeometry.js`): Proper directional cone from caster toward a specific aim-point, with 53Â° half-angle, segment intersection, and distance filtering
- **AI cone aim-picking** (`tactics.js`): `evalBreathWeapon` and `evalDragonFear` now aim cones at each enemy and pick the direction hitting the most hostiles
- **Shared breath/fear pool**: `dragonResource.uses` pool so breath weapon and Dragon Fear share the same limited resource
- **16 new cone tests** in `aoeGeometry.test.js`

#### Batch 2 â€” Reaction Framework (Fixes #5-9)
- **Core reaction framework** (`EncounterRunner.js`): `processReactions()` fires on single-attack-hit, multiattack, and spell-cast triggers; `applyReaction()` resolves each reaction type
- **Cutting Words**: Bard reaction to reduce attack/damage rolls by 1d10
- **Counterspell**: Cancel enemy spells, higher slots auto-succeed, lower slots require ability check
- **Silvery Barbs**: Force reroll on successful saves/attacks
- **24 new reaction tests** in `reactions.test.js`

#### Batch 3 â€” New Spells (Fixes #10-14)
- **Sleep** (`spells.js` + `ActionResolver.js`): HP-pool area spell, upcasts with +2d8/level, sorts targets by HP ascending, skips undead/charm-immune. Wake-on-damage integrated into `removeCharmedHPOnDamage`.
- **Polymorph** (`spells.js` + `ActionResolver.js` + `TurnMenu.js`): Enemy â†’ sheep (1 HP, WIS save with Legendary Resistance check). Self â†’ picks highest-HP beast form (Giant Ape 157 HP, AC 12, Fist 3d10+6 multiattack 2). Stores `prePolymorphState` with all original stats. Revert on 0 HP with overflow damage.
- **Faerie Fire** (`spells.js` + `ActionResolver.js`): DEX save, concentration, grants advantage on attacks against affected targets. Cleanup on concentration break removes condition from all targets.
- **Greater Invisibility** (`tactics.js`): Proactive evaluator for self-buffing before combat engagement
- **Polymorph revert wiring**: `checkPolymorphRevert` helper called from `resolveAttack`, `resolveMultiattack`, and `applySpellDamage`. `breakConcentration` handles both Faerie Fire (remove from all) and Polymorph (full stat revert).
- **TurnMenu self-targeting**: Polymorph can target both enemies AND self via `self_buff`/`enemy_nerf` special tags
- **19 new spell tests** in `newSpells.test.js`

#### Batch 4 â€” Simulation (Fix #15)
- Full test suite: **1262 tests, 0 failures** across all 19 test files
- Simulation: 379 builds Ã— 8 scenarios Ã— 10 sims runs cleanly
- Top build avg scores: ~33 (within variance range of Round 2's ~38 with only 10 sims)

### Test Debugging Highlights
- `optionId` vs `id` on menu options (menu uses `optionId`)
- `spellDef.save` must be `{ ability: 'wis', negatesAll: true }` not a string
- Average-mode dice: d12=6.5, d8=4.5 (fractional), advantage yields max(10,10)=10 (no benefit)
- Giant Ape (157 HP) > T-Rex (136 HP) for self-polymorph selection
- Brute `multiattack: 2` caused double-attack in revert test

### Files Modified (Round 3)

- `server/combat/engine-v2/TurnMenu.js` â€” Self+enemy targeting for Polymorph
- `server/combat/engine-v2/EncounterRunner.js` â€” Full reaction framework (Batch 2)
- `server/combat/ai/tactics.js` â€” Cone aim-picking, all new spell evaluators, reaction evaluators
- `server/combat/data/spells.js` â€” Sleep, Faerie Fire, Silvery Barbs, Polymorph definitions
- `server/combat/data/buildConverter.js` â€” LORE_BARD_KNOWN spell list, dragonFear.uses
- `server/combat/engine-v2/TacticsAdapter.js` â€” makeAdaptedReactionAI

- `server/combat/engine-v2/__tests__/reactions.test.js` â€” 24 new tests (NEW FILE)
- `server/combat/engine-v2/__tests__/aoeGeometry.test.js` â€” 16 new cone tests

### Cumulative Progress
| Round | Win Rate | Top Build Avg | Tests |
|-------|---------|---------------|-------|
| Baseline | 0.68% | 17.9 | 869 |
| Round 1 | 2.87% | 30.6 | ~920 |
| Round 2 | 3.13% | 38.0 | 1250 |
| Round 3 | â€” | ~33 (10-sim variance) | 1262 |

### What Was Learned
1. Average-mode dice produce fractional values (d12=6.5) which flow through damageâ†’overkillâ†’restored HP calculations. Tests must account for this.
2. Menu options use `optionId` not `id` â€” important for all test mocking
3. Self-targeting spells need special TurnMenu handling via `special` tags since `isHostile` filtering would exclude the caster
4. Polymorph is the most complex spell implemented â€” requires stat storage, revert on damage, revert on concentration break, and proper cleanup of conditions

### Emotional Response
Round 3 was the most ambitious round yet â€” 15 fixes across 4 batches, spanning cone geometry, a full reaction framework, and 4 major new spells. The Polymorph implementation alone required touching 5 different code paths. Proud that every piece was test-driven and the full suite passes cleanly.

## Interaction: Deep Bug Research â€” Polymorph Combat Engine Issues

### What Was Discussed
Creator asked for a thorough investigation of 4 critical bugs in the DnD combat engine related to Polymorph mechanics:
1. Polymorph revert not triggering on spell damage
2. Concentration "expiring" after 10 rounds
3. Dragon keeps dodging after revert
4. Evaluator tactic conditions for enemy vs self polymorph

### What Was Done
Comprehensive code analysis across 6 files: ActionResolver.js, EncounterRunner.js, TurnMenu.js, TacticsAdapter.js, tactics.js, and spells.js. Traced execution paths for spell damage â†’ polymorph revert, concentration timer mechanics, AI decision â†’ TurnMenu validation â†’ adapter fallback, and evaluator priority ordering.

### Bugs Identified

**Bug 1 â€” Three sub-bugs:**
- 1a: `applySpellDamage` calls `checkPolymorphRevert` but silently drops the revert logs (line 887-889). State change works, log is invisible.
- 1b: Enemy polymorph doesn't override `saves`, `legendaryResistance`, or ability modifiers. Sheep uses dragon's WIS save (+4) and 3 Legendary Resistance auto-passes.
- 1c: Enemy `prePolymorphState` missing `flying: target.flying` (line 712-721). Self-polymorph preState includes it (line 757-765). After revert, flying dragon permanently grounded.

**Bug 2:** Polymorph `duration: 10` in spells.js (line 807) = 10 rounds = 1 minute, not the correct 1 hour (600 rounds). Concentration timer forces expiry at round 10.

**Bug 3:** TacticsAdapter (line 340-344) falls back to Dodge when v1 AI decision can't match a TurnMenu option. After revert, dragon loses `flying` (Bug 1c), can't reach flying bard (30ft altitude > 10ft melee range), so multiattack never matches â†’ permanent dodge loop.

**Bug 4:** `evalEnemyPolymorph` and `evalSelfPolymorph` are condition-based (not scored). Enemy polymorph is tried first (line 963) and fires against high-HP non-humanoid enemies. Self-polymorph (line 964) fires only when HP < 60% or 2+ enemies in melee and enemy polymorph conditions aren't met.

### What Was Learned
- The polymorph state machine has asymmetric save/restore between enemy and self paths â€” enemy path is less thorough
- The TacticsAdapter dodge fallback silently masks action matching failures, making bugs hard to detect from combat logs alone
- The combination of missing logs + missing flying restore creates a scenario that LOOKS like "sheep survived 10 rounds" but is actually "sheep died early, dragon reverted silently, dragon grounded and can't fight"

### Decisions Made
- Identified 5 specific fix locations across ActionResolver.js, spells.js, and TacticsAdapter.js
- No code changes made yet â€” research only per Creator's request
